# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I found **24 Java source files** across the Kafka codebase that implement the log segment and index architecture:

### Core Components:
1. **LogSegment** - The main class managing individual log segment files
2. **Index Classes** - OffsetIndex, TimeIndex, TransactionIndex (implementing different file formats), AbstractIndex (base class), and LazyIndex (lazy-loading wrapper)
3. **LogConfig** - Validates log-level configuration properties
4. **LogLoader** - Orchestrates log recovery from disk during startup

### Checkpoint & Recovery:
5. **Checkpoint Files** - OffsetCheckpointFile, LeaderEpochCheckpointFile, and supporting infrastructure for persisting recovery points
6. **LeaderEpochFileCache** - Maintains leader epoch information for correctness
7. **ProducerStateManager** - Manages idempotency state and rebuilds during recovery

### Log Management:
8. **UnifiedLog & LocalLog** - High-level and low-level log APIs
9. **LogSegments** - Thread-safe segment collection management
10. **LogFileUtils** - Filename conventions and utilities

All files are located in `github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` under the `storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/` package hierarchy.

The core components include:\\n\\n**Log Segment Implementation**: LogSegment (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java) is the main class that represents a single log segment file. It manages the actual log data storage, index lookups, and recovery operations.\\n\\n**Index File Format**: The index architecture consists of three types of indices:\\n- OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java): Maps logical offsets to physical file positions using 8-byte entries (4-byte relative offset + 4-byte file position)\\n- TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java): Maps timestamps to offsets using 12-byte entries (8-byte timestamp + 4-byte relative offset)\\n- TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java): Tracks aborted transactions for transactional message filtering\\n- AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java): Base class providing common index functionality including memory-mapped file handling and sanity checks\\n- LazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java): Lazy-loading wrapper for index files to optimize memory usage\\n\\n**Log Configuration**: LogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) handles log-level configuration validation and property management, including segment size, index interval, retention policies, and cleanup policies.\\n\\n**Log Recovery from Checkpoints**: The log recovery process uses multiple checkpoint files:\\n- OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java): Persists recovery points and log start offsets to enable recovery without replaying entire logs\\n- OffsetCheckpoints (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpoints.java): Interface for checkpoint operations\\n- LazyOffsetCheckpoints (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LazyOffsetCheckpoints.java): Lazy-loads checkpoint files for performance\\n- CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler.java): Handles checkpoint persistence with failure handling\\n- LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java): Persists leader epoch information for correctness guarantees\\n\\n**Log Loading and Recovery**: The recovery process is orchestrated by:\\n- LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java): Loads log segments from disk, performs recovery for segments above the recovery point, validates indices, and rebuilds producer state\\n- LoadedLogOffsets (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LoadedLogOffsets.java): Data class containing the recovered log start offset and recovery point\\n- LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java): Caches leader epoch information and validates log truncations\\n- ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java): Manages producer idempotency state snapshots and recovery\\n- ProducerStateManagerConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManagerConfig.java): Configuration for producer state management\\n\\n**Log Management**: The overall log structure is managed by:\\n- UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java): High-level log API that coordinates with LocalLog for segment operations\\n- LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java): Manages the local log segments, provides append/read operations, and coordinates recovery\\n- LogSegments (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegments.java): Thread-safe navigable map of LogSegment instances\\n- LogFileUtils (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogFileUtils.java): Utility for generating segment filenames following Kafka's naming conventions\\n- LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java): Manages log cleanup including cleaner-offset-checkpoint\\n\\n**Supporting Components**:\\n- CleanedTransactionMetadata (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/CleanedTransactionMetadata.java): Tracks transaction state during log cleaning\\n- RemoteIndexCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/RemoteIndexCache.java): Caches indices for remote log segments in tiered storage scenarios\\n\\nThe architecture ensures durability through checkpoint files that record recovery points, log start offsets, and leader epochs. On startup, the LogLoader reads these checkpoints to determine which segments need recovery, validates index files, and rebuilds in-memory structures like the producer state and leader epoch cache. This allows Kafka brokers to recover from unclean shutdowns efficiently without replaying the entire log.\"\n}\n",

The core components include:\\n\\n**Log Segment Implementation**: LogSegment (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java) is the main class that represents a single log segment file. It manages the actual log data storage, index lookups, and recovery operations.\\n\\n**Index File Format**: The index architecture consists of three types of indices:\\n- OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java): Maps logical offsets to physical file positions using 8-byte entries (4-byte relative offset + 4-byte file position)\\n- TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java): Maps timestamps to offsets using 12-byte entries (8-byte timestamp + 4-byte relative offset)\\n- TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java): Tracks aborted transactions for transactional message filtering\\n- AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java): Base class providing common index functionality including memory-mapped file handling and sanity checks\\n- LazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java): Lazy-loading wrapper for index files to optimize memory usage\\n\\n**Log Configuration**: LogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) handles log-level configuration validation and property management, including segment size, index interval, retention policies, and cleanup policies.\\n\\n**Log Recovery from Checkpoints**: The log recovery process uses multiple checkpoint files:\\n- OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java): Persists recovery points and log start offsets to enable recovery without replaying entire logs\\n- OffsetCheckpoints (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpoints.java): Interface for checkpoint operations\\n- LazyOffsetCheckpoints (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LazyOffsetCheckpoints.java): Lazy-loads checkpoint files for performance\\n- CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler.java): Handles checkpoint persistence with failure handling\\n- LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java): Persists leader epoch information for correctness guarantees\\n\\n**Log Loading and Recovery**: The recovery process is orchestrated by:\\n- LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java): Loads log segments from disk, performs recovery for segments above the recovery point, validates indices, and rebuilds producer state\\n- LoadedLogOffsets (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LoadedLogOffsets.java): Data class containing the recovered log start offset and recovery point\\n- LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java): Caches leader epoch information and validates log truncations\\n- ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java): Manages producer idempotency state snapshots and recovery\\n- ProducerStateManagerConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManagerConfig.java): Configuration for producer state management\\n\\n**Log Management**: The overall log structure is managed by:\\n- UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java): High-level log API that coordinates with LocalLog for segment operations\\n- LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java): Manages the local log segments, provides append/read operations, and coordinates recovery\\n- LogSegments (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegments.java): Thread-safe navigable map of LogSegment instances\\n- LogFileUtils (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogFileUtils.java): Utility for generating segment filenames following Kafka's naming conventions\\n- LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java): Manages log cleanup including cleaner-offset-checkpoint\\n\\n**Supporting Components**:\\n- CleanedTransactionMetadata (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/CleanedTransactionMetadata.java): Tracks transaction state during log cleaning\\n- RemoteIndexCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/RemoteIndexCache.java): Caches indices for remote log segments in tiered storage scenarios\\n\\nThe architecture ensures durability through checkpoint files that record recovery points, log start offsets, and leader epochs. On startup, the LogLoader reads these checkpoints to determine which segments need recovery, validates index files, and rebuilds in-memory structures like the producer state and leader epoch cache. This allows Kafka brokers to recover from unclean shutdowns efficiently without replaying the entire log.\"\n}\n",
